4.conclusions 1
althoughunlikelytobeasolutiontoproblemsassociatedwithplasticwaste,a 1
phasinginofbiobasedbiodegradablepolymersmayhelptomaintainthehealthofthe 1
environment.variousmicrobialstrainshavebeendetectedthatconvertplasticpolymersto 1

toworkintheenvironmentorinindustrialprocesses,theexploitationofmicrobesfor 1
degradationofplasticswouldbeaneco-friendlymethod.alogicalstep,represented 1
bythepresentandotherstudies,istoidentifythetypesandofnaturalplastic- 1
degradingmicrobes.microbesandtheenzymesthattheyproducerepresentamajorarea 1
ofcurrentresearchinconnectionwithapotentialuseinthebioremediationofplasticrefuse. 1
however,thediversityofknownenzymesandmicrobesactingonsyntheticpolymersis 1
stillratherlimited[ 1

temperatures.samplingtookplaceduringthewintermonthsinnorway.thepresent 1
